{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-09-16 13:04:15","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:04:15","title":"Retro Inspired Illustrator for Lightspeed EP","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/ELE1uC82muI/retro-inspired-illustrator-lightspeed-ep","description":"Retro Inspired Illustrator for Lightspeed EP\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/retro-inspired-illustrator-lightspeed-ep\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_lightspeed.jpg\" width=\"1760\" height=\"1364\" alt=\"Retro Inspired Illustrator for Lightspeed EP\" title=\"Retro Inspired Illustrator for Lightspeed EP\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.10.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/joaorm\">João Marques</a> shared this retro inspired illustration and motion design project for the Lightspeed EP. In September of 2019, DJ/producer KURA released a new EP on Spinnin' Records entitled 'Lightspeed'. A really energetic and fierce EP, especially the title track ‘Lightspeed’, a big room production with a hard drop and cool sample snippets. </p>\n\n<p>The artwork for this was inspired by the musical elements present on this EP, exploring impactful and colorful retro-futuristic visuals in the same way the tracks on the EP explore various elements from the past and future of electronic dance music. </p>\n\n<p>The cover art also features four distinct symbols to represent each of the EP's tracks: a lightning for ‘Lightspeed’, a crystal ball for ‘Jinx’, a flame for 'Burn', and a vinyl record for ‘New School’. Each of these symbols was also animated as part of the promotional material for social media.</p>\n\n<h3>EP artwork</h3>\n\n<p><img href=\"http://www.oritoor.com\">ori toor</a> humorously calls his playful, creative and beautiful illustration & doodle series. At first, I was even questioning why he calls it 'Gibberish' but just by reading his bio, you quickly understand why. Basically, Ori is a master of his craft at doodling sketches without any planning just improvising. This is something I dearly appreciate, it's fun to just let go of things and let your mind go free to be creative. We are featuring his set titled: 'Gibberish Dark Mode (And one light)' but I would totally suggest you visit his <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/oritoor\">Behance</a> for more of his delightful style.</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"http://www.oritoor.com\">http://www.oritoor.com</a></li>\n\t<li><a class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/seryozhaparshakov\">Seryozha Parshakov</a> is an artist based in Moscow, Russian Federation. I wanted to share about his 'Ancient Future' series which is an art series showcasing an abstract exploration of masks combining ancient and modern textures. I totally feel a dystopian feel to these, especially the texture and the 'true tone black color' as a baseline. But at the same time because of its ancient visual approach from past centuries, it's definitely something worth featuring on abdz. We have featured his most recent set of the series but I would totally suggest checking his <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/seryozhaparshakov\">Behance</a> for more.</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"http://o-f.cc\">http://o-f.cc</a></li>\n\t<li><a Carrier of Time\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/motion-design-monday-carrier-time\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_taiwan.png\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" alt=\"Motion Design Monday! Carrier of Time\" title=\"Motion Design Monday! Carrier of Time\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.14.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>It’s Motion Design Monday and we would love to share the amazing project that <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/Children-C\">Children Chiu </a>shared titled Carrier of Time. It was done using Houdini and Redshift and it’s simply beautiful. It was created to promote Taiwan. Since the Age of Discovery, Taiwan has been irradiated with diverse cultures. This history makes Taiwan merge different cultures, and refract them into beautiful shadows. As the carrier of our history and culture, these historical national treasures were born in its own era and shaped the beauty of this land, describes Children Chiu on the original post.</p>\n\n<p>Time is a river, carrying light moving forward, continuously shaping who we are everyday. The shadows of time are the accumulation of our history and culture.</p>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/450730204\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1680px;margin:auto;\">\n<div style=\"left: 0; 13:04:15","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:04:15","title":"Branding Concept for Mies Van Der Rohe Architecture Firm","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/xeJCmzMdFnA/branding-concept-mies-van-der-rohe-architecture-firm","description":"Branding Concept for Mies Van Der Rohe Architecture Firm\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/branding-concept-mies-van-der-rohe-architecture-firm\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_mvdr.gif\" width=\"1800\" height=\"1100\" alt=\"Branding Concept for Mies Van Der Rohe Architecture Firm\" title=\"Branding Concept for Mies Van Der Rohe Architecture Firm\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.15.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/lucasgilturner\">Lucas Gil-Turner</a> created a tribute project  to one of his favorite architects (Mies van der Rohe). The idea was to imagine what a brand would look like for such an emblematic and representative architecture firm, says Lucas. What a great idea and great execution. This is a great example of using a passion as a motivator to explore/learn new things. The byproduct of that, you can get some awesome work on your portfolio. </p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>Starting from the premise of the main partner of \"less is more\", the concept behind this proposal is characterised by the simplicity of the structural elements, the geometric composition and the absence of ornamental elements. The whole system is based on proportions and sobriety. The logo has two versions: a more extended one that contains the full name and a reduced version where only the initials would appear for the cases in which it is more difficult to apply. The color palette consists of three different grays (light, medium, and dark) plus black and white. The typeface used is Din Pro, whose origin is found in the design published in 1931 by the German Institute for Standardisation (Din 1451). It was created primarily for industrial uses and technical drawings. Due to its readability, simplicity, and no frills, it became very popular for general signage use.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"Image may contain: man, person and Zhang</a> shared an awesome branding and illustration project with us for UNI Music Academy, which is the first of its kind music learning academy for kids ages six through teen. They are focused on providing a safe, inspiring, and empowering space for children to identify, develop, and refine their music senses. </p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>They challenged us to create a branding that elevates UNI music with Retro, the 70s, 80s, Illustration, Universe, and a bold style while communicating the creative and playful of their new style of music Pub","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/DTmyxjanGuk/branding-full-visual-identity-la-mala-pub","description":"Branding & Full Visual Identity for La Mala Pub\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/branding-full-visual-identity-la-mala-pub\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_mala.jpg\" width=\"1400\" height=\"935\" alt=\"Branding & Full Visual Identity for La Mala Pub\" title=\"Branding & Full Visual Identity for La Mala Pub\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.09.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://estudionuar.com/la-mala\">Estudio Nuar</a> shared a beautiful branding project for La Mala Pub. Right in the heart of Palermo, La Mala Pub leads Buenos Aires nightlife. Only a few months after opening, it became so trending that generated the need for more space. In consequence, an extra space was attached and Malita was created. It was a joint work with the architecture team to design the new identity for this space and then generate all the graphic interventions and signage applications. </p>\n\n<p>La Mala in Spanish means “Bad Girl” and that’s what triggered the visual imaginary, with all these really empowered girls, a bit vintage but updated with the vibrant colors, the contemporary phrases and the spacial mood, meaning she’s from outer space. </p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>We created this multifaceted character who represents La Mala but also every girl who goes there. Apart from the posters, which are one of the main characters, we worked a lot on the neon signs, together with the architecture team, as they were very important taking into consideration it’s a night pub and the lighting is fundamental.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_italian_designers.png\" width=\"2640\" height=\"1992\" alt=\"Italians Who Design: a repository to showcase Italians work to the world\" title=\"Italians Who Design: a repository to showcase Italians work to the world\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.09.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://italianswho.design/\">Italians Who Design</a> is a showcase of the most talented Italian designers out there. It aims to help people find notable and relevant voices to inspire others, increase and diversify their network and (why not?) to find someone to work with. There is a number of Italian designers that are working abroad designing products used by millions that are less known in the international scenario as they deserve.</p>\n\n<p><img alt=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/QkXUHnAnHC75yCAqFeoDSdswUdFzaVwd3dgygbEy6gMvYWYdMy9f8hG9s4otWZM7dKmfuSqKyZyy_NF7r1fcC5VOnzYnaUKLB5j1larspV7orZqdVUllJ73jRBmNMGuhafl8hqax\" src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/IxlHcjXO37B85or191O_zH131Akff9H07yRA-IQupGt5HVk37wUct5O395nZ7-8yK4gLI_TFmAQBUJoIeH3QjpjCq1YJeKeRPDibwmbDx8VHR_yDVH6wXcSR-dE4JaJghHEdg167GSL_gBPj7w\" /></p>\n\n<p>It’s inspired by Fabricio Teixeira’s article about ‘Brazilians Who Design’, an amazing project to showcase talented Brazilian design portfolios. However, you may have already faced similar websites, for example:</p>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://womenwho.design/\">Women Who Design</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"http://www.28blacks.com/\">28 Black Designers</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.latinxswhodesign.com/\">Latinx Who Design</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://uruguayanswho.design/\">Uruguayans Who Design</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://filipinos-who-design.webflow.io/\">Filipinos Who Design</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://peopleofcraft.com/\">People Of Craft</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://indianswhodesign.in/\">Indians Who Design</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.apiwho.design/\">Asian & Pacific Islanders Who Design</a></li>\n</ul><p>We have a long history of amazing Italian designers and our style is well known all around the world, so it made sense to create Italians Who Design.</p>\n\n<h3>Sharing and evolving</h3>\n\n<p>Starting from the first shares, we discussed a lot about how detailed and atomic we should go by listing the different roles. We decided to keep it as simple as possible with the hope that people's links (and portfolios) will help tell the full story, so we started with these categories: UX/Product, Branding, Graphic, Motion, and Illustration.</p>\n\n<p>We are still discussing, but it is quite possible that we will add a few other categories as Writing, Industrial, and Research as the list grows. There is still a long way to go before we reach a final state but this is the funny part about building something new.</p>\n\n<h3>About</h3>\n\n<p>Italians Who Design was created by Andrea Paci and Alessandro Greco, but the inspiration came from Brazilians Who Design, we really want to thank Fabricio and Zeh who helped us a lot before the launch.</p>\n\n<p>We hope you enjoy the site and please, if you know Italian designers that are not yet part of the list, nominate them filling the form here or share the link to our <a href=\"https://italianswho.design/\">website</a>.</p>\n</div><div
